commit 3f0d55a16d437f82b8faa75af598f93a82d2fe78
Author: Tim Reynolds <s-reynot@cthulu.jax.org>
Date:   Tue Nov 1 18:02:35 2016 -0400

    Alter the geneset annotation behavior on edit geneset page
    
    The tree view now only allows users to add new annotations of the types
    "Manual Association" or "Manual Rejection" to the geneset. Previous behavior
    allowed users to remove annotations or add new ones of whatever reference type
    was selected. "Manual Rejection" will be used in cases where a user has
    positively deselected an annotation and it should not be reselected (e.g. in
    the case of running the automated annotator again).
    
    Added two new functions to geneweaverdb for updating a current annotation
    reference type and another for determining if a particular term is annotated to
    a geneset.

commit 0cc3f1dc023bdae949491bcd704dd674e08a1456
Author: Tim Reynolds <s-reynot@cthulu.jax.org>
Date:   Thu Oct 27 13:17:53 2016 -0400

    Fix single geneset upload gene handling
    
    The single GS upload page will now accept genes with improper capitalization.
    Prior to this, e.g. uploading a gene Shank3 for humans would not work since the
    human gene is SHANK3.
    The update makes use of case insensitive searching and the CI postgres index.
    
    Single GS upload will also preserve the proper capitalization when displaying
    genes on the view/edit geneset page. This way genes don't show up like
    'shank3'.
